</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Reports Fiscal 2024 Third Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Lowering Guidance in Continued Challenging Environment; Provides Strategic Update </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Third quarter financial highlights </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I></I>Third quarter earnings per share (EPS)* was $0.40 compared to earnings per share of $0.14 in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter which included a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment of pharmacy license intangible assets in Boots UK </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Adjusted EPS** was $0.63, down 36.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis compared to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including a $0.24 impact from lower sale-leaseback gains, a challenging U.S. retail environment, and recent pharmacy industry trends </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Third quarter sales increased 2.6&nbsp;percent year-over-year to $36.4&nbsp;billion, up 2.5&nbsp;percent on a
constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Fiscal 2024 guidance<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> </I></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Lowering fiscal 2024 adjusted EPS** guidance to $2.80 to $2.95 reflecting challenging pharmacy industry trends
and a worse-than-expected U.S. consumer environment </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Update on strategic review </I></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Finalizing significant multiyear footprint optimization program to close certain underperforming U.S. stores
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Launching U.S. Retail Pharmacy action plan to invest in and deliver an improved customer and patient experience
across channels </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Aligning U.S. Pharmacy and Healthcare organizations for enhanced <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">go-to-market</FONT></FONT> capabilities </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Simplifying and focusing the U.S. Healthcare portfolio </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD, Ill. &#151; June&nbsp;27, 2024 &#151; Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the third quarter of
fiscal 2024, which ended May&nbsp;31, 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Chief Executive Officer Tim Wentworth said: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We continue to face a difficult operating environment, including persistent pressures on the U.S. consumer and the impact of recent marketplace dynamics
which have eroded pharmacy margins. Our results and outlook reflect these headwinds, despite solid performance in both our International and U.S. Healthcare segments. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Informed by our strategic review, we are focused on improving our core business: retail pharmacy, which is central to the future of healthcare. We are
addressing critical issues with urgency and working to unlock opportunities for growth. Many of these actions will take time, but I am confident that we have the right team and the right strategy to lead a business turnaround for the Walgreens that
our customers and patients need.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:26%">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on
a forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort and the Company is unable to address the probable
significance of the unavailable information. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">&#147;Adjusted,&#148; &#147;constant currency&#148; and free cash flow
amounts are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. See the appendix to this release for a discussion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, including a reconciliation to the most closely
correlated GAAP measure. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Third Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA third quarter sales increased 2.6&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $36.4&nbsp;billion, an increase of
2.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting sales growth across all segments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third quarter operating income was $111&nbsp;million compared
to an operating loss of $477&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, an increase of $588&nbsp;million, which reflects lapping a $431&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment of
pharmacy license intangible assets in Boots UK in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted operating income** was $613&nbsp;million, a decrease of 36.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis reflecting lower
sale-leaseback gains and softer U.S. retail and pharmacy performance, partly offset by cost savings initiatives and improved profitability in the U.S. Healthcare segment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net earnings in the third quarter were $344&nbsp;million compared to net earnings of $118&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter, an increase of $225&nbsp;million reflecting higher operating income. Adjusted net earnings** were $545&nbsp;million, down 36.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower adjusted operating income**. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">EPS in the third quarter was $0.40 compared to $0.14 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting an increase of $0.26.
Adjusted EPS** was $0.63, reflecting a decrease of 36.6&nbsp;percent, or $0.36 on both a reported and constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by
operating activities was $605&nbsp;million in the third quarter and free cash flow** was $334&nbsp;million, a $778&nbsp;million increase compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, each driven primarily by phasing and
optimization of working capital. The increase in free cash flow also benefited from decreased capital expenditures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Fiscal 2024 <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Year-to-Date</FONT></FONT> Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales in the first nine months of fiscal 2024 increased
6.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period to $110.1&nbsp;billion, an increase of 5.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting growth across all segments. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating loss in the first nine months of fiscal 2024 was $13.1&nbsp;billion compared to an operating loss of $6.4&nbsp;billion in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, an increase in operating loss of $6.7&nbsp;billion. Operating loss in the current period reflects a $12.4&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charge related to
VillageMD goodwill, which resulted in a $5.8&nbsp;billion charge attributable to WBA, net of tax and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-controlling</FONT> interest. Operating loss in the current period also reflects a $455&nbsp;million <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charge related to certain long-lived assets in the U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment. Prior year operating loss reflects a $6.8&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> charge for
opioid-related claims and litigation and a $431&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment of pharmacy license intangible assets in Boots UK. Adjusted operating income** was $2.2&nbsp;billion, a decrease of
31.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis reflecting a challenging U.S. retail environment, reimbursement pressure and lower sale-leaseback gains, partly offset by cost savings and improved profitability in the U.S. Healthcare segment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net loss for the first nine months of fiscal 2024 was $5.6&nbsp;billion compared to a net loss of $2.9&nbsp;billion in the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, an increase in net loss of $2.7&nbsp;billion, reflecting the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges and lapping a $1.5&nbsp;billion gain on sales of Cencora and
Option Care Health shares last year. Adjusted net earnings** decreased 24.9&nbsp;percent, or $712&nbsp;million to $2.2&nbsp;billion, down 25.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower adjusted operating income** partly offset by a
lower adjusted effective tax** rate due to the recognition of deferred tax assets in foreign jurisdictions in the second quarter. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Loss per share for the first nine months of fiscal 2024 was $6.53 compared to a loss per share of $3.36 in
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, an increase in loss per share of $3.17. Adjusted EPS** decreased 24.9&nbsp;percent, or $0.83, to $2.49, reflecting a decrease of 25.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash used for operating activities was $314&nbsp;million in the first nine months of fiscal 2024 and free cash flow** was negative $1.1&nbsp;billion, a
$1.2&nbsp;billion decrease compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, with each driven primarily by lower earnings, $780&nbsp;million in higher payments related to legal matters and phasing of working capital. The
decrease in free cash flow was partly offset by $497&nbsp;million in decreased capital expenditures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business Segments </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>U.S. Retail Pharmacy </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment had third quarter sales of $28.5&nbsp;billion, an increase of 2.3&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter driven entirely by comparable pharmacy sales, partly offset by a retail decline. Comparable sales increased 3.5&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pharmacy sales increased 4.4&nbsp;percent and comparable pharmacy sales increased 5.7&nbsp;percent compared to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, benefiting from higher branded drug inflation and script growth. Comparable prescriptions filled in the third quarter, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents
increased 1.6&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter while comparable prescriptions excluding immunizations increased 1.7&nbsp;percent. Total prescriptions filled in the quarter, including immunizations,
adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents was 306.4&nbsp;million, an increase of 0.5&nbsp;percent versus the prior year quarter. Pharmacy margin was negatively impacted by brand mix impacts and reimbursement pressure.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail sales decreased 4.0&nbsp;percent and comparable retail sales decreased 2.3&nbsp;percent compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting a challenging retail environment and continued channel shift. Retail margin was negatively affected by increased promotional activity and higher shrink levels. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted operating income** decreased 47.9&nbsp;percent to $501&nbsp;million compared to $1.0&nbsp;billion in the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting lower sale and leaseback gains, a challenging retail environment and reimbursement pressure, net of procurement savings, partly offset by cost savings initiatives. </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The U.S. Healthcare segment had third quarter sales of $2.1&nbsp;billion, an increase of 7.6&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, led by VillageMD and Shields. VillageMD grew 7&nbsp;percent, reflecting additional lives in risk and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">fee-for-service.</FONT></FONT>
Shields grew 24&nbsp;percent, driven by growth within existing partnerships. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating loss was $220&nbsp;million compared to an operating loss of
$522&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted operating loss**, which excludes certain costs related to amortization of acquired intangible assets and stock compensation expense, was $22&nbsp;million
compared to $172&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted EBITDA** of $23&nbsp;million improved by
$136&nbsp;million versus the prior year quarter and represents the second consecutive quarter of positive adjusted EBITDA** for the segment, driven by cost discipline and growth from VillageMD and Shields. </P>

discuss the third quarter results beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time today, June&nbsp;27, 2024. A live simulcast as well as related presentation materials will be available through WBA&#146;s investor relations website at:
<B>https://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com</B>. A replay of the conference will be archived on the website for at least 12 months after the event. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">ENDS </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Notes to Editors:
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walgreens Boots
Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is an integrated healthcare, pharmacy and retail leader serving millions of customers and patients every day, with a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">170-year</FONT> heritage of caring for communities. A trusted, global
innovator in retail pharmacy with approximately 12,500 locations across the U.S., Europe and Latin America, WBA plays a critical role in the healthcare ecosystem. The Company is reimagining local healthcare and well-being for all as part of its
purpose &#150; to create more joyful lives through better health. Through dispensing medicines, improving access to a wide range of health services, providing high quality health and beauty products and offering anytime, anywhere convenience across
its digital platforms, WBA is shaping the future of healthcare. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA employs more than 330,000 people and has a presence in eight countries through its
portfolio of consumer brands: Walgreens, Boots, Duane Reade, the No7 Beauty Company and Benavides in Mexico. Additionally, WBA has a portfolio of healthcare-focused investments located in several countries, including China and the U.S. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. WBA has been
recognized for its commitment to being an inclusive workplace. In fiscal 2023, the Company received a score of 100 from the Human Rights Campaign&#146;s Corporate Equality Index, scored 100&nbsp;percent on the Disability Equality Index for
disability inclusion and was named Disability:IN&#146;s 2023 Employer of the Year. In addition, WBA has been recognized for its commitment to operating sustainably as the company is an index component of the Dow Jones Sustainability Indices (DJSI).
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">More Company information is available at www.walgreensbootsalliance.com. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following information provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under
the SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The Company has provided the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not calculated or presented in accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and
presented in accordance with GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because
management has evaluated the Company&#146;s financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the Company from period to period and trends in the Company&#146;s historical
operating results. The Company also uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures as a basis for certain compensation programs it sponsors. These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial
measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press release. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates to the most directly comparable GAAP financial
measures on a forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of
forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet occurred, are out of the Company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, such as unusual <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> charges, tax expenses, and
material litigation expenses, and that would impact diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the Company is unable to address the probable significance of the
unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially from the corresponding GAAP financial measures.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Constant currency </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company also presents certain
information related to current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the
foreign currency exchange rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The Company presents such constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the U.S. reporting in currencies other than the U.S.
dollar and such presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Comparable sales </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The nine months ended May&nbsp;31, 2024 comparable sales and prescriptions filled figures for the Company exclude the benefit of this year&#146;s leap day.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy and International segments, Comparable sales are defined as sales from stores that have been open for at
least twelve consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to looting or store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster, in the past twelve months as well as <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. Comparable sales in constant currency exclude wholesale sales in Germany and sales from dispositions in the current period. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include
digitally initiated sales online or through mobile applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable sales for the first twelve months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable sales for the first twelve months
after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT>
equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively. The method of calculating comparable sales
varies across the retail industry and our method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same as other retailers&#146; methods. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With respect to
the International segment, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales, are presented on a constant currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion
above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company considers certain metrics, such as comparable sales (in constant currency), comparable pharmacy sales (in constant currency), comparable retail
sales (in constant currency), comparable number of prescriptions, comparable prescriptions excluding immunizations, and comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions to be key performance indicators because the
Company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the
Company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP
financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other companies. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Impairment of goodwill, intangibles and long-lived assets recognized in the nine months ended May&nbsp;31, 2024
resulted from the interim goodwill impairment assessment for the VillageMD reporting unit. These charges do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance
because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses
and Impairment of goodwill within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities recorded in Operating income (loss) within the Consolidated Condensed Statement of Earnings. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance, stock-based compensation, employee transaction success bonuses, and
other integration related exit and disposal charges. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs are significantly impacted by the
timing and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, inventory
valuation adjustments and stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed
technology and contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The
revenue generated by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular
period unless an intangible asset becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of
Earnings. The stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustment reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense
recognized in excess of the original grant date fair value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and
are not reflective of normal operating activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

legal proceedings, including legal defense costs. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation

litigation settlement frameworks and certain other legal matters. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on cost of sales as if the U.S. Retail Pharmacy
segment inventory is accounted for using <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix,
and manufacturer pricing practices, which may be impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the Company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> adjustments on the underlying derivative instruments reflects the Company&#146;s operational performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">post-tax</FONT> (loss) earnings from other equity method
investments consist of the proportionate share of certain equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments. These charges are recorded in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Post-tax</FONT> (loss) earnings from other equity method investments within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of
Earnings. Although the Company may have shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity method investments are not intended to imply that the
Company has direct control over their operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these
equity method investees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Due to the anti-dilutive effect resulting from periods where the Company reports a net loss, the impact of
potentially dilutive securities on the per share amounts has been omitted from the calculation of weighted-average common shares outstanding for diluted net loss per common share. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company reconciles Adjusted EBITDA for the U.S. Healthcare segment to Operating loss as the closest GAAP
measure for the segment profitability. The Company does not measure Net earnings attributable to Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. for its segments. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Impairment of goodwill, intangibles and long-lived assets recognized in the nine months ended May&nbsp;31, 2024
resulted from the interim goodwill impairment assessment for the VillageMD reporting unit. These charges do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance
because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses
and Impairment of goodwill within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, inventory
valuation adjustments and stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed
technology and contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The
revenue generated by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular
period unless an intangible asset becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of
Earnings. The stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustment reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense
recognized in excess of the original grant date fair value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and
are not reflective of normal operating activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities recorded in Operating income (loss) within the Consolidated Condensed Statement of Earnings. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance, stock-based compensation, employee transaction success bonuses, and
other integration related exit and disposal charges. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs are significantly impacted by the
timing and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These
charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring
activity. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Includes GAAP stock-based compensation expense excluding expenses related to acquisition-related amortization
and acquisition-related costs. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property,
plant and equipment (capital expenditures), plus acquisition related payments and incremental pension payments made in that period. This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not
deduct the payments required for debt service and other contractual obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to the
Consolidated Condensed Statement of Cash Flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the three months ended May&nbsp;31, 2023, the Company paid $101&nbsp;million to settle liability
classified share-based payment awards related to acquiring the remaining 45% equity interest in CareCentrix. In addition to the $101&nbsp;million, during the nine months ended May&nbsp;31, 2023, the Company paid $335&nbsp;million to settle liability
classified share-based payment awards related to acquiring the remaining 30% equity interest in Shields. The Company also paid <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> compensation costs related to VillageMD&#146;s acquisition of Summit. The
payments are not indicative of normal operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the three and nine months ended May&nbsp;31, 2024, the Company made incremental pension contributions of
$7M and $386M, respectively, to the Boots Plan as part of the Trustee&#146;s acquisition of a bulk annuity policy (the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Buy-In&#148;)</FONT> from Legal and General. The payments are not indicative of normal
operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">#&#8195;#&#8195;#&#8195;#&#8195;# </P>
